# WWDC 2018 Keynote

## Summary
WWDC 2018 Keynote

## Info
* Featured
* WWDC 2018 - Session 101 - iOS, macOS, tvOS, watchOS
* https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/101/

이 비범한 포유동물들은](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/101/?time=54) [본능에 의해 유목민이 되어버리죠](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/101/?time=58) [본능에 의해 유목민이 되어버리죠](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/101/?time=58) [바로 개발자 종족입니다](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/101/?time=62) [우리에게 더 친숙한 이름은 바로](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/101/?time=67) [개발자이지만요](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/101/?time=70) [11개월 하고도 보름 간의
겨울잠은 쉽지 않았을 것이며](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/101/?time=77) [이제 태양이 작열하는군요](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/101/?time=82) [동굴 안에 서식하던 야행성 종족이

쉽지 않을 수 있겠군요](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/101/?time=124) [일부에게는 친해지는 것이

개발자 커뮤니티 여러분과 함께](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/101/?time=532) [고객들에게
